結論：DosimeTron在多樣的提示配置中自主執行複雜的劑量計算管道，並在臨床可接受的處理時間內與OpenDose3D達成高劑量一致性，顯示了代理AI在PET/CT中進行患者特定蒙特卡羅劑量計算的可行性。

##### **CRFT: Consistent-Recurrent Feature Flow Transformer for Cross-Modal Image Registration**
2604.05689v1 by Xuecong Liu, Mengzhu Ding, Zixuan Sun, Zhang Li, Xichao Teng

We present Consistent-Recurrent Feature Flow Transformer (CRFT), a unified coarse-to-fine framework based on feature flow learning for robust cross-modal image registration. CRFT learns a modality-independent feature flow representation within a transformer-based architecture that jointly performs feature alignment and flow estimation. The coarse stage establishes global correspondences through multi-scale feature correlation, while the fine stage refines local details via hierarchical feature fusion and adaptive spatial reasoning. To enhance geometric adaptability, an iterative discrepancy-guided attention mechanism with a Spatial Geometric Transform (SGT) recurrently refines the flow field, progressively capturing subtle spatial inconsistencies and enforcing feature-level consistency. This design enables accurate alignment under large affine and scale variations while maintaining structural coherence across modalities. Extensive experiments on diverse cross-modal datasets demonstrate that CRFT consistently outperforms state-of-the-art registration methods in both accuracy and robustness. Beyond registration, CRFT provides a generalizable paradigm for multimodal spatial correspondence, offering broad applicability to remote sensing, autonomous navigation, and medical imaging. Code and datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/NEU-Liuxuecong/CRFT.

摘要：我們提出了一種一致性-重複特徵流Transformer（CRFT），這是一個基於特徵流學習的統一粗到細框架，用於穩健的跨模態影像配準。<lb/>CRFT在基於Transformer的架構中學習模態獨立的特徵流表示，該架構共同執行特徵對齊和流場估計。<lb/>粗略階段通過多尺度特徵相關性建立全局對應，而細緻階段則通過層次特徵融合和自適應空間推理來細化局部細節。<lb/>為了增強幾何適應性，一種迭代的差異引導注意機制與空間幾何變換（SGT）反復細化流場，逐步捕捉微妙的空間不一致並強化特徵級一致性。<lb/>這種設計使得在大仿射和尺度變化下能夠準確對齊，同時保持跨模態的結構一致性。<lb/>在各種跨模態數據集上的廣泛實驗表明，CRFT在準確性和穩健性方面始終超越了最先進的配準方法。<lb/>除了配準之外，CRFT還提供了一種可泛化的多模態空間對應範式，對遙感、自主導航和醫學影像等領域具有廣泛的應用性。<lb/>代碼和數據集可在 https://github.com/NEU-Liuxuecong/CRFT 上公開獲得。

##### **Analogical Reasoning as a Doctor: A Foundation Model for Gastrointestinal Endoscopy Diagnosis**
2604.05649v1 by Peixi Peng, Housheng Xie, Yanling Wei, Guangcong Ruan, Xiaoyang Zou, Qian Cao, Yongjian Nian, Guoyan Zheng

Gastrointestinal diseases impose a growing global health burden, and endoscopy is a primary tool for early diagnosis. However, routine endoscopic image interpretation still suffers from missed lesions and limited efficiency. Although AI-assisted diagnosis has shown promise, existing models often lack generalizability, adaptability, robustness, and scalability because of limited medical data, domain shift, and heterogeneous annotations. To address these challenges, we develop RATNet, a foundation model for gastrointestinal endoscopy imaging based on analogical reasoning. RATNet acquires and transfers knowledge from heterogeneous expert annotations across five gastrointestinal endoscopy datasets through a cyclic pre-training strategy. Its architecture consists of an encoder, a relevance-knowledge acquisition and transfer (RAT) module, a projector, and a multi-task head, and supports fine-tuning, linear probing, and zero-shot transfer. Evaluations show that RATNet outperforms existing foundation models, including GastroNet and GastroVision, across six scenarios: diagnosis of common gastrointestinal diseases, few-shot learning for rare diseases, zero-shot transfer to new medical sites, robustness under long-tailed disease distributions, adaptation to novel diseases, and privacy-preserving deployment via federated learning. Its advantage comes from an analogical reasoning mechanism that matches image-derived posterior knowledge to a learned prior knowledge base and transfers relative knowledge to guide diagnosis, improving generalization and resistance to bias. RATNet is open and cost-effective, supports automatic integration of heterogeneous annotations without manual label unification, and reduces data acquisition costs, making it a practical foundation for intelligent gastrointestinal diagnosis, especially in resource-limited settings.

摘要：腸胃疾病對全球健康造成日益增長的負擔，而內視鏡檢查是早期診斷的主要工具。<lb/>然而，常規的內視鏡影像解讀仍然面臨漏診和效率有限的問題。<lb/>儘管AI輔助診斷顯示出潛力，但現有模型往往缺乏普遍性、適應性、穩健性和可擴展性，原因在於醫療數據有限、領域轉移和異質標註。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們開發了RATNet，一個基於類比推理的腸胃內視鏡影像基礎模型。<lb/>RATNet通過循環預訓練策略從五個腸胃內視鏡數據集中獲取並轉移來自異質專家標註的知識。<lb/>其架構由編碼器、相關知識獲取與轉移（RAT）模塊、投影器和多任務頭組成，並支持微調、線性探測和零樣本轉移。<lb/>評估顯示，RATNet在六個場景中超越了現有的基礎模型，包括GastroNet和GastroVision：常見腸胃疾病的診斷、稀有疾病的少樣本學習、新醫療場地的零樣本轉移、在長尾疾病分佈下的穩健性、對新疾病的適應，以及通過聯邦學習實現的隱私保護部署。<lb/>其優勢來自於一種類比推理機制，該機制將影像衍生的後驗知識與學習的先驗知識庫相匹配，並轉移相對知識以指導診斷，從而提高了泛化能力和抗偏見能力。<lb/>RATNet是開放且具成本效益的，支持自動整合異質標註而無需手動標籤統一，並降低數據獲取成本，使其成為智能腸胃診斷的實用基礎，特別是在資源有限的環境中。

##### **Semantic-Topological Graph Reasoning for Language-Guided Pulmonary Screening**
2604.05620v1 by Chenyu Xue, Yiran Liu, Mian Zhou, Jionglong Su, Zhixiang Lu

Medical image segmentation driven by free-text clinical instructions is a critical frontier in computer-aided diagnosis. However, existing multimodal and foundation models struggle with the semantic ambiguity of clinical reports and fail to disambiguate complex anatomical overlaps in low-contrast scans. Furthermore, fully fine-tuning these massive architectures on limited medical datasets invariably leads to severe overfitting. To address these challenges, we propose a novel Semantic-Topological Graph Reasoning (STGR) framework for language-guided pulmonary screening. Our approach elegantly synergizes the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLaMA-3-V) with the zero-shot delineation of vision foundation models (MedSAM). Specifically, we introduce a Text-to-Vision Intent Distillation (TVID) module to extract precise diagnostic guidance. To resolve anatomical ambiguity, we formulate mask selection as a dynamic graph reasoning problem, where candidate lesions are modeled as nodes and edges capture spatial and semantic affinities. To ensure deployment feasibility, we introduce a Selective Asymmetric Fine-Tuning (SAFT) strategy that updates less than 1% of the parameters. Rigorous 5-fold cross-validation on the LIDC-IDRI and LNDb datasets demonstrates that our framework establishes a new state-of-the-art. Notably, it achieves an 81.5% Dice Similarity Coefficient (DSC) on LIDC-IDRI, outperforming leading LLM-based tools like LISA by over 5%. Crucially, our SAFT strategy acts as a powerful regularizer, yielding exceptional cross-fold stability (0.6% DSC variance) and paving the way for robust, context-aware clinical deployment.

摘要：醫學影像分割由自由文本臨床指示驅動，是計算機輔助診斷的一個關鍵前沿。然而，現有的多模態和基礎模型在臨床報告的語義模糊性方面掙扎，無法解釋低對比度掃描中的複雜解剖重疊。此外，對這些龐大架構在有限醫學數據集上進行完全微調，無疑會導致嚴重的過擬合。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了一種新穎的語義-拓撲圖推理（STGR）框架，用於語言引導的肺部篩查。我們的方法優雅地協同了大型語言模型（LLaMA-3-V）的推理能力與視覺基礎模型（MedSAM）的零-shot 描述。具體而言，我們引入了一個文本到視覺意圖蒸餾（TVID）模組，以提取精確的診斷指導。為了解決解剖模糊性，我們將掩膜選擇公式化為一個動態圖推理問題，其中候選病變被建模為節點，邊緣捕捉空間和語義親和性。為了確保部署的可行性，我們引入了一種選擇性非對稱微調（SAFT）策略，更新不到1%的參數。在LIDC-IDRI和LNDb數據集上進行的嚴格5折交叉驗證表明，我們的框架建立了一個新的最先進技術。值得注意的是，它在LIDC-IDRI上達到了81.5%的Dice相似係數（DSC），超過了領先的基於LLM的工具，如LISA，超出5%以上。關鍵是，我們的SAFT策略作為一種強大的正則化器，產生了卓越的交叉折穩定性（0.6%的DSC變異），為穩健的、上下文感知的臨床部署鋪平了道路。

##### **INTERACT: An AI-Driven Extended Reality Framework for Accesible Communication Featuring Real-Time Sign Language Interpretation and Emotion Recognition**
2604.05605v1 by Nikolaos D. Tantaroudas, Andrew J. McCracken, Ilias Karachalios, Evangelos Papatheou

Video conferencing has become central to professional collaboration, yet most platforms offer limited support for deaf, hard-of-hearing, and multilingual users. The World Health Organisation estimates that over 430 million people worldwide require rehabilitation for disabling hearing loss, a figure projected to exceed 700 million by 2050. Conventional accessibility measures remain constrained by high costs, limited availability, and logistical barriers, while Extended Reality (XR) technologies open new possibilities for immersive and inclusive communication. This paper presents INTERACT (Inclusive Networking for Translation and Embodied Real-Time Augmented Communication Tool), an AI-driven XR platform that integrates real-time speech-to-text conversion, International Sign Language (ISL) rendering through 3D avatars, multilingual translation, and emotion recognition within an immersive virtual environment. ##### **MO-RiskVAE: A Multi-Omics Variational Autoencoder for Survival Risk Modeling in Multiple MyelomaMO-RiskVAE**
2604.06267v1 by Zixuan Chen, Heng Zhang, YuPeng Qin, WenPeng Xing, Qiang Wang, Da Wang, Changting Lin, Meng Han

Multimodal variational autoencoders (VAEs) have emerged as a powerful framework for survival risk modeling in multiple myeloma by integrating heterogeneous omics and clinical data. However, when trained under survival supervision, standard latent regularization strategies often fail to preserve prognostically relevant variation, leading to unstable or overly constrained representations. Despite numerous proposed variants, it remains unclear which aspects of latent design fundamentally govern performance in this setting. In this work, we conduct a controlled investigation of latent modeling choices for multimodal survival prediction within a unified extension of the MyeVAE framework. By systematically isolating regularization scale, posterior geometry, and latent space structure under identical architectures and optimization protocols, we show that survival-driven training is primarily sensitive to the magnitude and structure of latent regularization rather than the specific divergence formulation. In particular, moderate relaxation of KL regularization consistently improves survival discrimination, while alternative divergence mechanisms such as MMD and HSIC provide limited benefit without appropriate scaling. We further demonstrate that structuring the latent space can improve alignment between learned representations and survival risk gradients. A hybrid continuous--discrete formulation based on Gumbel--Softmax enhances global risk ordering in the continuous latent subspace, even though stable discrete subtype discovery does not emerge under survival supervision. Guided by these findings, we instantiate a robust multimodal survival model, termed MO-RiskVAE, which consistently improves risk stratification over the original MyeVAE without introducing additional supervision or complex training heuristics.

摘要：多模態變分自編碼器（VAEs）已成為多發性骨髓瘤中生存風險建模的強大框架，通過整合異質的組學和臨床數據。然而，在生存監督下訓練時，標準的潛在正則化策略往往無法保留預後相關的變異，導致不穩定或過度約束的表示。儘管提出了許多變種，但在這種情況下，潛在設計的哪些方面根本上影響性能仍不清楚。在本研究中，我們對多模態生存預測中的潛在建模選擇進行了受控調查，並在MyeVAE框架的統一擴展下進行。通過在相同的架構和優化協議下系統地隔離正則化尺度、後驗幾何和潛在空間結構，我們表明生存驅動的訓練主要對潛在正則化的大小和結構敏感，而不是特定的散度公式。特別是，適度放鬆KL正則化始終能改善生存區分，而其他散度機制如MMD和HSIC在沒有適當縮放的情況下提供的好處有限。我們進一步展示了結構化潛在空間可以改善學習表示與生存風險梯度之間的對齊。基於Gumbel--Softmax的混合連續--離散公式在連續潛在子空間中增強了全局風險排序，即使在生存監督下穩定的離散亞型發現並未出現。根據這些發現，我們實現了一個穩健的多模態生存模型，稱為MO-RiskVAE，該模型在不引入額外監督或複雜訓練啟發式的情況下，始終改善了相對於原始MyeVAE的風險分層。

##### **From Retinal Evidence to Safe Decisions: RETINA-SAFE and ECRT for Hallucination Risk Triage in Medical LLMs**
2604.05348v1 by Zhe Yu, Wenpeng Xing, Meng Han

Hallucinations in medical large language models (LLMs) remain a safety-critical issue, particularly when available evidence is insufficient or conflicting. We study this problem in diabetic retinopathy (DR) decision settings and introduce RETINA-SAFE, an evidence-grounded benchmark aligned with retinal grading records, comprising 12,522 samples. RETINA-SAFE is organized into three evidence-relation tasks: E-Align (evidence-consistent), E-Conflict (evidence-conflicting), and E-Gap (evidence-insufficient). We further propose ECRT (Evidence-Conditioned Risk Triage), a two-stage white-box detection framework: Stage 1 performs Safe/Unsafe risk triage, and Stage 2 refines unsafe cases into contradiction-driven versus evidence-gap risks. ECRT leverages internal representation and logit shifts under CTX/NOCTX conditions, with class-balanced training for robust learning. Under evidence-grouped (not patient-disjoint) splits across multiple backbones, ECRT provides strong Stage-1 risk triage and explicit subtype attribution, improves Stage-1 balanced accuracy by +0.15 to +0.19 over external uncertainty and self-consistency baselines and by +0.02 to +0.07 over the strongest adapted supervised baseline, and consistently exceeds a single-stage white-box ablation on Stage-1 balanced accuracy. These findings support white-box internal signals grounded in retinal evidence as a practical route to interpretable medical LLM risk triage.

摘要：醫療大型語言模型（LLMs）中的幻覺仍然是一個安全關鍵問題，特別是在可用證據不足或相互矛盾的情況下。我們在糖尿病視網膜病變（DR）決策環境中研究這個問題，並介紹了RETINA-SAFE，這是一個與視網膜分級記錄對齊的基於證據的基準，包含12,522個樣本。RETINA-SAFE被組織為三個證據關係任務：E-Align（證據一致）、E-Conflict（證據衝突）和E-Gap（證據不足）。我們進一步提出ECRT（基於證據的風險分流），這是一個兩階段的白盒檢測框架：第一階段執行安全/不安全風險分流，第二階段將不安全案例細分為矛盾驅動和證據缺口風險。ECRT利用內部表示和在CTX/NOCTX條件下的logit變化，並進行類別平衡訓練以實現穩健學習。在跨多個骨幹的證據分組（而非患者不重疊）拆分下，ECRT提供強大的第一階段風險分流和明確的亞類別歸屬，將第一階段的平衡準確度提高了+0.15到+0.19，超過外部不確定性和自我一致性基線，並且比最強的適應性監督基線提高了+0.02到+0.07，並且在第一階段平衡準確度上持續超過單階段白盒消融。這些發現支持基於視網膜證據的白盒內部信號作為可解釋的醫療LLM風險分流的實用途徑。

##### **From Exposure to Internalization: Dual-Stream Calibration for In-context Clinical Reasoning**
2604.06262v1 by Chuang Zhao, Hongke Zhao, Xiaofang Zhou, Xiaomeng Li

Contextual clinical reasoning demands robust inference grounded in complex, heterogeneous clinical records. While state-of-the-art fine-tuning, in-context learning (ICL), and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) enable knowledge exposure, they often fall short of genuine contextual internalization: dynamically adjusting a model's internal representations to the subtle nuances of individual cases at inference time. To address this, we propose Dual-Stream Calibration (DSC), a test-time training framework that transcends superficial knowledge exposure to achieve deep internalization during inference. DSC facilitates input internalization by synergistically aligning two calibration streams. Unlike passive context exposure, the Semantic Calibration Stream enforces a deliberative reflection on core evidence, internalizing semantic anchors by minimizing entropy to stabilize generative trajectories. Simultaneously, the Structural Calibration Stream assimilates latent inferential dependencies through an iterative meta-learning objective. By training on specialized support sets at test-time, this stream enables the model to bridge the gap between external evidence and internal logic, synthesizing fragmented data into a coherent response. Our approach shifts the reasoning paradigm from passive attention-based matching to an active refinement of the latent inferential space. Validated against thirteen clinical datasets, DSC demonstrates superiority across three distinct task paradigms, consistently outstripping state-of-the-art baselines ranging from training-dependent models to test-time learning frameworks.

摘要：上下文臨床推理需要基於複雜且異質的臨床記錄進行穩健的推斷。雖然最先進的微調、上下文學習（ICL）和檢索增強生成（RAG）能夠實現知識的曝光，但它們往往無法實現真正的上下文內化：在推斷時動態調整模型的內部表徵以適應個別案例的細微差別。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了雙流校準（DSC），這是一個測試時訓練框架，超越了表面的知識曝光，以在推斷過程中實現深層內化。DSC通過協同對齊兩個校準流來促進輸入內化。與被動的上下文曝光不同，語義校準流強調對核心證據的深思熟慮，通過最小化熵來內化語義錨點，以穩定生成軌跡。同時，結構校準流通過迭代的元學習目標同化潛在的推理依賴關係。通過在測試時對專門的支持集進行訓練，這一流使模型能夠彌合外部證據與內部邏輯之間的差距，將零散數據合成為一致的回應。我們的方法將推理範式從被動的基於注意力的匹配轉變為對潛在推理空間的主動精煉。在對十三個臨床數據集進行驗證後，DSC在三個不同的任務範式中顯示出優越性，始終超越從依賴訓練的模型到測試時學習框架的最先進基準。

##### **Improving Clinical Trial Recruitment using Clinical Narratives and Large Language Models**
2604.05190v1 by Ziyi Chen, Mengxian Lyu, Cheng Peng, Yonghui Wu

Screening patients for enrollment is a well-known, labor-intensive bottleneck that leads to under-enrollment and, ultimately, trial failures. Recent breakthroughs in large language models (LLMs) offer a promising opportunity to use artificial intelligence to improve screening. This study systematically explored both encoder- and decoder-based generative LLMs for screening clinical narratives to facilitate clinical trial recruitment. We examined both general-purpose LLMs and medical-adapted LLMs and explored three strategies to alleviate the "Lost in the Middle" issue when handling long documents, including 1) Original long-context: using the default context windows of LLMs, 2) NER-based extractive summarization: converting the long document into summarizations using named entity recognition, 3) RAG: dynamic evidence retrieval based on eligibility criteria. The 2018 N2C2 Track 1 benchmark dataset is used for evaluation. Our experimental results show that the MedGemma model with the RAG strategy achieved the best micro-F1 score of 89.05%, outperforming other models. Generative LLMs have remarkably improved trial criteria that require long-term reasoning across long documents, whereas trial criteria that span a short piece of context (e.g., lab tests) show incremental improvements. The real-world adoption of LLMs for trial recruitment must consider specific criteria for selecting among rule-based queries, encoder-based LLMs, and generative LLMs to maximize efficiency within reasonable computing costs.

摘要：篩選患者以進行登記是一個眾所周知的勞動密集型瓶頸，導致登記不足，最終導致試驗失敗。最近在大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的突破提供了一個有希望的機會，利用人工智慧來改善篩選。本研究系統性地探索了基於編碼器和解碼器的生成性LLMs，以篩選臨床敘事，促進臨床試驗招募。我們檢查了通用LLMs和醫療適應LLMs，並探索了三種策略來緩解處理長文件時的「迷失於中間」問題，包括 1) 原始長上下文：使用LLMs的默認上下文窗口，2) 基於NER的提取性摘要：使用命名實體識別將長文檔轉換為摘要，3) RAG：基於資格標準的動態證據檢索。2018年N2C2 Track 1基準數據集用於評估。我們的實驗結果顯示，採用RAG策略的MedGemma模型達到了最佳的微F1分數89.05%，超越了其他模型。生成性LLMs顯著改善了需要在長文檔中進行長期推理的試驗標準，而跨越短上下文片段（例如，實驗室測試）的試驗標準則顯示出增量改善。將LLMs實際應用於試驗招募時，必須考慮在基於規則的查詢、基於編碼器的LLMs和生成性LLMs之間選擇的具體標準，以最大化在合理計算成本內的效率。

##### **Modality-Aware and Anatomical Vector-Quantized Autoencoding for Multimodal Brain MRI**
2604.05171v1 by Mingjie Li, Edward Kim, Yue Zhao, Ehsan Adeli, Kilian M. Pohl

Learning a robust Variational Autoencoder (VAE) is a fundamental step for many deep learning applications in medical image analysis, such as MRI synthesizes. Existing brain VAEs predominantly focus on single-modality data (i.e., T1-weighted MRI), overlooking the complementary diagnostic value of other modalities like T2-weighted MRIs. Here, we propose a modality-aware and anatomically grounded 3D vector-quantized VAE (VQ-VAE) for reconstructing multi-modal brain MRIs. Called NeuroQuant, it first learns a shared latent representation across modalities using factorized multi-axis attention, which can capture relationships between distant brain regions. It then employs a dual-stream 3D encoder that explicitly separates the encoding of modality-invariant anatomical structures from modality-dependent appearance. Next, the anatomical encoding is discretized using a shared codebook and combined with modality-specific appearance features via Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM) during the decoding phase. This entire approach is trained using a joint 2D/3D strategy in order to account for the slice-based acquisition of 3D MRI data. Extensive experiments on two multi-modal brain MRI datasets demonstrate that NeuroQuant achieves superior reconstruction fidelity compared to existing VAEs, enabling a scalable foundation for downstream generative modeling and cross-modal brain image analysis.

摘要：學習一個穩健的變分自編碼器（VAE）是許多深度學習應用於醫學影像分析中的基本步驟，例如MRI合成。現有的腦部VAE主要集中於單一模態數據（即T1加權MRI），忽視了其他模態如T2加權MRI的互補診斷價值。在這裡，我們提出了一種模態感知且具有解剖學基礎的3D向量量化VAE（VQ-VAE），用於重建多模態腦部MRI。這種名為NeuroQuant的模型首先使用因子化的多軸注意力學習跨模態的共享潛在表示，能夠捕捉遠端腦區之間的關係。然後，它採用一個雙流3D編碼器，明確地將模態不變的解剖結構的編碼與模態依賴的外觀分開。接下來，使用共享代碼本對解剖編碼進行離散化，並在解碼階段通過特徵線性調制（FiLM）將其與模態特定的外觀特徵結合。整個方法使用聯合2D/3D策略進行訓練，以考慮3D MRI數據的切片基礎獲取。在兩個多模態腦部MRI數據集上的大量實驗表明，NeuroQuant在重建保真度方面優於現有的VAE，為下游生成建模和跨模態腦影像分析提供了可擴展的基礎。

##### **SE-Enhanced ViT and BiLSTM-Based Intrusion Detection for Secure IIoT and IoMT Environments**
2604.06254v1 by Afrah Gueriani, Hamza Kheddar, Ahmed Cherif Mazari, Seref Sagiroglu, Onur Ceran

With the rapid growth of interconnected devices in Industrial and Medical Internet of Things (IIoT and MIoT) ecosystems, ensuring timely and accurate detection of cyber threats has become a critical challenge. This study presents an advanced intrusion detection framework based on a hybrid Squeeze-and-Excitation Attention Vision Transformer-Bidirectional Long Short-Term Memory (SE ViT-BiLSTM) architecture. In this design, the traditional multi-head attention mechanism of the Vision Transformer is replaced with Squeeze-and-Excitation attention, and integrated with BiLSTM layers to enhance detection accuracy and computational efficiency. The proposed model was trained and evaluated on two real-world benchmark datasets; EdgeIIoT and CICIoMT2024; both before and after data balancing using the Synthetic Minority Over-sampling Technique (SMOTE) and RandomOverSampler. Experimental results demonstrate that the SE ViT-BiLSTM model outperforms existing approaches across multiple metrics. Before balancing, the model achieved accuracies of 99.11% (FPR: 0.0013%, latency: 0.00032 sec/inst) on EdgeIIoT and 96.10% (FPR: 0.0036%, latency: 0.00053 sec/inst) on CICIoMT2024. After balancing, performance further improved, reaching 99.33% accuracy with 0.00035 sec/inst latency on EdgeIIoT and 98.16% accuracy with 0.00014 sec/inst latency on CICIoMT2024.

摘要：隨著工業和醫療物聯網 (IIoT 和 MIoT) 生態系統中互聯設備的快速增長，確保及時和準確地檢測網絡威脅已成為一個關鍵挑戰。這項研究提出了一種基於混合擠壓與激勵注意力視覺Transformer-雙向長短期記憶 (SE ViT-BiLSTM) 架構的先進入侵檢測框架。在這一設計中，視覺Transformer的傳統多頭注意力機制被擠壓與激勵注意力所取代，並與 BiLSTM 層集成以提高檢測準確性和計算效率。所提出的模型在兩個真實世界基準數據集上進行了訓練和評估；EdgeIIoT 和 CICIoMT2024；在使用合成少數類別過採樣技術 (SMOTE) 和隨機過採樣器 (RandomOverSampler) 進行數據平衡之前和之後。實驗結果表明，SE ViT-BiLSTM 模型在多個指標上超越了現有方法。在平衡之前，該模型在 EdgeIIoT 上達到了 99.11% 的準確率 (FPR: 0.0013%，延遲: 0.00032 秒/實例) 和在 CICIoMT2024 上達到了 96.10% 的準確率 (FPR: 0.0036%，延遲: 0.00053 秒/實例)。在平衡之後，性能進一步提高，在 EdgeIIoT 上達到了 99.33% 的準確率，延遲為 0.00035 秒/實例，在 CICIoMT2024 上達到了 98.16% 的準確率，延遲為 0.00014 秒/實例。

##### **Uncertainty-Guided Latent Diagnostic Trajectory Learning for Sequential Clinical Diagnosis**
2604.05116v1 by Xuyang Shen, Haoran Liu, Dongjin Song, Martin Renqiang Min

Clinical diagnosis requires sequential evidence acquisition under uncertainty. However, most Large Language Model (LLM) based diagnostic systems assume fully observed patient information and therefore do not explicitly model how clinical evidence should be sequentially acquired over time. Even when diagnosis is formulated as a sequential decision process, it is still challenging to learn effective diagnostic trajectories. This is because the space of possible evidence-acquisition paths is relatively large, while clinical datasets rarely provide explicit supervision information for desirable diagnostic paths. To this end, we formulate sequential diagnosis as a Latent Diagnostic Trajectory Learning (LDTL) framework based on a planning LLM agent and a diagnostic LLM agent. For the diagnostic LLM agent, diagnostic action sequences are treated as latent paths and we introduce a posterior distribution that prioritizes trajectories providing more diagnostic information. The planning LLM agent is then trained to follow this distribution, encouraging coherent diagnostic trajectories that progressively reduce uncertainty. Experiments on the MIMIC-CDM benchmark demonstrate that our proposed LDTL framework outperforms existing baselines in diagnostic accuracy under a sequential clinical diagnosis setting, while requiring fewer diagnostic tests. Furthermore, ablation studies highlight the critical role of trajectory-level posterior alignment in achieving these improvements.

摘要：臨床診斷需要在不確定性下進行連續的證據獲取。<lb/>然而，大多數基於大型語言模型 (LLM) 的診斷系統假設患者信息是完全可觀察的，因此並未明確建模臨床證據應如何隨時間順序獲取。<lb/>即使將診斷表述為一個連續的決策過程，學習有效的診斷軌跡仍然具有挑戰性。<lb/>這是因為可能的證據獲取路徑空間相對較大，而臨床數據集很少提供對理想診斷路徑的明確監督信息。<lb/>為此，我們將連續診斷公式化為一個基於規劃 LLM 代理和診斷 LLM 代理的潛在診斷軌跡學習 (LDTL) 框架。<lb/>對於診斷 LLM 代理，診斷行動序列被視為潛在路徑，我們引入一個後驗分佈，優先考慮提供更多診斷信息的軌跡。<lb/>然後，規劃 LLM 代理被訓練以遵循這一分佈，鼓勵連貫的診斷軌跡，逐步減少不確定性。<lb/>在 MIMIC-CDM 基準上的實驗表明，我們提出的 LDTL 框架在連續臨床診斷設置下的診斷準確性上超過了現有的基準，同時需要更少的診斷測試。<lb/>此外，消融研究突顯了軌跡級後驗對齊在實現這些改進中的關鍵作用。

##### **MedGemma 1.5 Technical Report**
2604.05081v1 by Andrew Sellergren, Chufan Gao, Fereshteh Mahvar, Timo Kohlberger, Fayaz Jamil, Madeleine Traverse, Alberto Tono, Bashir Sadjad, Lin Yang, Charles Lau, Liron Yatziv, Tiffany Chen, Bram Sterling, Kenneth Philbrick, Richa Tiwari, Yun Liu, Madhuram Jajoo, Chandrashekar Sankarapu, Swapnil Vispute, Harshad Purandare, Abhishek Bijay Mishra, Sam Schmidgall, Tao Tu, Anil Palepu, Chunjong Park, Tim Strother, Rahul Thapa, Yong Cheng, Preeti Singh, Kat Black, Yossi Matias, Katherine Chou, Avinatan Hassidim, Kavi Goel, Joelle Barral, Tris Warkentin, Shravya Shetty, Dale Webster, Sunny Virmani, David F. Steiner, Can Kirmizibayrak, Daniel Golden

We introduce MedGemma 1.5 4B, the latest model in the MedGemma collection. MedGemma 1.5 expands on MedGemma 1 by integrating additional capabilities: high-dimensional medical imaging (CT/MRI volumes and histopathology whole slide images), anatomical localization via bounding boxes, multi-timepoint chest X-ray analysis, and improved medical document understanding (lab reports, electronic health records). We detail the innovations required to enable these modalities within a single architecture, including new training data, long-context 3D volume slicing, and whole-slide pathology sampling. Compared to MedGemma 1 4B, MedGemma 1.5 4B demonstrates significant gains in these new areas, improving 3D MRI condition classification accuracy by 11% and 3D CT condition classification by 3% (absolute improvements). In whole slide pathology imaging, MedGemma 1.5 4B achieves a 47% macro F1 gain. Additionally, it improves anatomical localization with a 35% increase in Intersection over Union on chest X-rays and achieves a 4% macro accuracy for longitudinal (multi-timepoint) chest x-ray analysis. Beyond its improved multimodal performance over MedGemma 1, MedGemma 1.5 improves on text-based clinical knowledge and reasoning, improving by 5% on MedQA accuracy and 22% on EHRQA accuracy. It also achieves an average of 18% macro F1 on 4 different lab report information extraction datasets (EHR Datasets 2, 3, 4, and Mendeley Clinical Laboratory Test Reports). Taken together, MedGemma 1.5 serves as a robust, open resource for the community, designed as an improved foundation on which developers can create the next generation of medical AI systems. Resources and tutorials for building upon MedGemma 1.5 can be found at https://goo.gle/MedGemma.

摘要：我們介紹 MedGemma 1.5 4B，MedGemma 系列中的最新模型。MedGemma 1.5 在 MedGemma 1 的基礎上擴展了額外的功能：高維度醫學影像（CT/MRI 體積和組織病理全片影像）、通過邊界框進行的解剖定位、多時間點胸部 X 光分析，以及改進的醫學文件理解（實驗室報告、電子健康記錄）。我們詳細說明了在單一架構內啟用這些模式所需的創新，包括新的訓練數據、長上下文 3D 體積切片和全片病理取樣。與 MedGemma 1 4B 相比，MedGemma 1.5 4B 在這些新領域顯示出顯著的增益，提高了 3D MRI 病情分類的準確性 11% 和 3D CT 病情分類的準確性 3%（絕對提升）。在全片病理影像中，MedGemma 1.5 4B 實現了 47% 的宏觀 F1 增益。此外，它在胸部 X 光的交集比（Intersection over Union）上提高了 35% 的解剖定位準確性，並在縱向（多時間點）胸部 X 光分析中達到了 4% 的宏觀準確率。除了在多模態性能上優於 MedGemma 1 之外，MedGemma 1.5 在基於文本的臨床知識和推理方面也有所改進，MedQA 準確性提高了 5%，EHRQA 準確性提高了 22%。它在 4 個不同的實驗室報告信息提取數據集（EHR Datasets 2、3、4 和 Mendeley Clinical Laboratory Test Reports）上也達到了平均 18% 的宏觀 F1。綜合來看，MedGemma 1.5 作為一個強大的開放資源服務於社區，旨在成為開發者創建下一代醫療 AI 系統的改進基礎。關於基於 MedGemma 1.5 構建的資源和教程，可以在 https://goo.gle/MedGemma 找到。

##### **This Treatment Works, Right? Evaluating LLM Sensitivity to Patient Question Framing in Medical QA**
2604.05051v1 by Hye Sun Yun, Geetika Kapoor, Michael Mackert, Ramez Kouzy, Wei Xu, Junyi Jessy Li, Byron C. Wallace

Patients are increasingly turning to large language models (LLMs) with medical questions that are complex and difficult to articulate clearly. However, LLMs are sensitive to prompt phrasings and can be influenced by the way questions are worded. Ideally, LLMs should respond consistently regardless of phrasing, particularly when grounded in the same underlying evidence. We investigate this through a systematic evaluation in a controlled retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) setting for medical question answering (QA), where expert-selected documents are used rather than retrieved automatically. We examine two dimensions of patient query variation: question framing (positive vs. negative) and language style (technical vs. plain language). We construct a dataset of 6,614 query pairs grounded in clinical trial abstracts and evaluate response consistency across eight LLMs. Our findings show that positively- and negatively-framed pairs are significantly more likely to produce contradictory conclusions than same-framing pairs. This framing effect is further amplified in multi-turn conversations, where sustained persuasion increases inconsistency. We find no significant interaction between framing and language style. Our results demonstrate that LLM responses in medical QA can be systematically influenced through query phrasing alone, even when grounded in the same evidence, highlighting the importance of phrasing robustness as an evaluation criterion for RAG-based systems in high-stakes settings.

摘要：患者越來越多地尋求大型語言模型 (LLMs) 來解答複雜且難以清晰表達的醫療問題。<lb/>然而，LLMs 對提示的措辭非常敏感，並且可能受到問題表述方式的影響。<lb/>理想情況下，LLMs 應該無論措辭如何都能一致回應，特別是在基於相同的基本證據時。<lb/>我們通過在一個受控的檢索增強生成 (RAG) 環境中對醫療問題回答 (QA) 進行系統評估來研究這一點，該環境中使用的是專家選擇的文檔，而不是自動檢索的。<lb/>我們考察患者查詢變異的兩個維度：問題框架（正面與負面）和語言風格（技術性與通俗語言）。<lb/>我們構建了一個包含 6,614 對查詢的數據集，這些查詢基於臨床試驗摘要，並評估八個 LLM 的回應一致性。<lb/>我們的發現顯示，正面和負面框架的對比組比同框架組更可能產生矛盾的結論。<lb/>這種框架效應在多輪對話中進一步加強，持續的說服會增加不一致性。<lb/>我們沒有發現框架與語言風格之間有顯著的相互作用。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，在醫療 QA 中，LLM 的回應可以僅通過查詢措辭系統性地受到影響，即使基於相同的證據，這突顯了措辭穩健性作為高風險環境中 RAG 基於系統的評估標準的重要性。

##### **Learning, Potential, and Retention: An Approach for Evaluating Adaptive AI-Enabled Medical Devices**
2604.04878v1 by Alexis Burgon, Berkman Sahiner, Nicholas A Petrick, Gene Pennello, Ravi K Samala

This work addresses challenges in evaluating adaptive artificial intelligence (AI) models for medical devices, where iterative updates to both models and evaluation datasets complicate performance assessment. We introduce a novel approach with three complementary measurements: learning (model improvement on current data), potential (dataset-driven performance shifts), and retention (knowledge preservation across modification steps), to disentangle performance changes caused by model adaptations versus dynamic environments. Case studies using simulated population shifts demonstrate the approach's utility: gradual transitions enable stable learning and retention, while rapid shifts reveal trade-offs between plasticity and stability. These measurements provide practical insights for regulatory science, enabling rigorous assessment of the safety and effectiveness of adaptive AI systems over sequential modifications.

摘要：這項工作針對評估醫療設備的自適應人工智慧（AI）模型所面臨的挑戰，因為模型和評估數據集的迭代更新使性能評估變得複雜。我們提出了一種新穎的方法，包含三個互補的測量指標：學習（模型在當前數據上的改進）、潛力（基於數據集的性能變化）和保留（在修改步驟中知識的保存），以區分由模型適應與動態環境引起的性能變化。使用模擬人口變化的案例研究展示了該方法的實用性：逐漸的過渡促進了穩定的學習和保留，而快速的變化則揭示了可塑性與穩定性之間的權衡。這些測量指標為監管科學提供了實用的見解，使得能夠對自適應AI系統在連續修改過程中的安全性和有效性進行嚴格評估。

##### **A Clinical Point Cloud Paradigm for In-Hospital Mortality Prediction from Multi-Level Incomplete Multimodal EHRs**
2604.04614v2 by Bohao Li, Tao Zou, Junchen Ye, Yan Gong, Bowen Du

Deep learning-based modeling of multimodal Electronic Health Records (EHRs) has become an important approach for clinical diagnosis and risk prediction. However, due to diverse clinical workflows and privacy constraints, raw EHRs are inherently multi-level incomplete, including irregular sampling, missing modalities, and sparse labels. These issues cause temporal misalignment, modality imbalance, and limited supervision. Most existing multimodal methods assume relatively complete data, and even methods designed for incompleteness usually address only one or two of these issues in isolation. As a result, they often rely on rigid temporal/modal alignment or discard incomplete data, which may distort raw clinical semantics. To address this problem, we propose HealthPoint (HP), a unified clinical point cloud paradigm for multi-level incomplete EHRs. HP represents heterogeneous clinical events as points in a continuous 4D space defined by content, time, modality, and case. To model interactions between arbitrary point pairs, we introduce a Low-Rank Relational Attention mechanism that efficiently captures high-order dependencies across these four dimensions. We further develop a hierarchical interaction and sampling strategy to balance fine-grained modeling and computational efficiency. Built on this framework, HP enables flexible event-level interaction and fine-grained self-supervision, supporting robust modality recovery and effective use of unlabeled data. Experiments on large-scale EHR datasets for risk prediction show that HP consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance and strong robustness under varying degrees of incompleteness.

摘要：基於深度學習的多模態電子健康紀錄（EHRs）建模已成為臨床診斷和風險預測的重要方法。<lb/>然而，由於多樣的臨床工作流程和隱私限制，原始EHR本質上是多層次不完整的，包括不規則取樣、缺失模態和稀疏標籤。<lb/>這些問題導致時間錯位、模態不平衡和有限的監督。<lb/>大多數現有的多模態方法假設數據相對完整，即使是針對不完整性設計的方法通常僅獨立解決其中一到兩個問題。<lb/>因此，它們往往依賴於僵化的時間/模態對齊或丟棄不完整數據，這可能會扭曲原始臨床語義。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了HealthPoint（HP），一種統一的多層次不完整EHR的臨床點雲範式。<lb/>HP將異質的臨床事件表示為在由內容、時間、模態和案例定義的連續4D空間中的點。<lb/>為了建模任意點對之間的相互作用，我們引入了一種低秩關係注意機制，能有效捕捉這四個維度之間的高階依賴性。<lb/>我們進一步開發了一種分層互動和取樣策略，以平衡細粒度建模和計算效率。<lb/>基於這一框架，HP實現了靈活的事件級互動和細粒度自我監督，支持穩健的模態恢復和有效利用未標記數據。<lb/>在大型EHR數據集上進行的風險預測實驗表明，HP在不同程度的不完整性下始終實現了最先進的性能和強大的穩健性。

##### **AI Agents Under EU Law**
2604.04604v1 by Luca Nannini, Adam Leon Smith, Michele Joshua Maggini, Enrico Panai, Sandra Feliciano, Aleksandr Tiulkanov, Elena Maran, James Gealy, Piercosma Bisconti

AI agents - i.e. AI systems that autonomously plan, invoke external tools, and execute multi-step action chains with reduced human involvement - are being deployed at scale across enterprise functions ranging from customer service and recruitment to clinical decision support and critical infrastructure management. The EU AI Act (Regulation 2024/1689) regulates these systems through a risk-based framework, but it does not operate in isolation: providers face simultaneous obligations under the GDPR, the Cyber Resilience Act, the Digital Services Act, the Data Act, the Data Governance Act, sector-specific legislation, the NIS2 Directive, and the revised Product Liability Directive. This paper provides the first systematic regulatory mapping for AI agent providers integrating (a) draft harmonised standards under Standardisation Request M/613 to CEN/CENELEC JTC 21 as of January 2026, (b) the GPAI Code of Practice published in July 2025, (c) the CRA harmonised standards programme under Mandate M/606 accepted in April 2025, and (d) the Digital Omnibus proposals of November 2025. We present a practical taxonomy of nine agent deployment categories mapping concrete actions to regulatory triggers, identify agent-specific compliance challenges in cybersecurity, human oversight, transparency across multi-party action chains, and runtime behavioral drift. We propose a twelve-step compliance architecture and a regulatory trigger mapping connecting agent actions to applicable legislation. We conclude that high-risk agentic systems with untraceable behavioral drift cannot currently satisfy the AI Act's essential requirements, and that the provider's foundational compliance task is an exhaustive inventory of the agent's external actions, data flows, connected systems, and affected persons.

摘要：AI 代理 - 即自主規劃、調用外部工具並執行多步驟行動鏈的 AI 系統，並減少人類參與 - 正在大規模部署於企業功能中，涵蓋從客戶服務和招聘到臨床決策支持和關鍵基礎設施管理等領域。歐盟 AI 法案（條例 2024/1689）通過風險基礎框架對這些系統進行監管，但並不是孤立運作：提供者面臨 GDPR、網絡韌性法、數字服務法、數據法、數據治理法、行業特定立法、NIS2 指令以及修訂的產品責任指令下的同時義務。本文提供了針對 AI 代理提供者的首個系統性監管映射，整合了 (a) 截至 2026 年 1 月的 CEN/CENELEC JTC 21 標準化請求 M/613 下的草擬統一標準，(b) 2025 年 7 月發布的 GPAI 行為準則，(c) 2025 年 4 月接受的 M/606 授權下的 CRA 統一標準計劃，以及 (d) 2025 年 11 月的數字綜合提案。我們提出了一個實用的九類代理部署分類法，將具體行動映射到監管觸發點，識別在網絡安全、人類監督、跨多方行動鏈的透明度以及運行時行為漂移方面的代理特定合規挑戰。我們提出了一個十二步合規架構和一個監管觸發映射，將代理行動與適用立法相連接。我們得出結論，高風險的代理系統如果存在無法追蹤的行為漂移，當前無法滿足 AI 法案的基本要求，而提供者的基礎合規任務是對代理的外部行動、數據流、連接系統和受影響人員進行全面清查。

##### **Ruling Out to Rule In: Contrastive Hypothesis Retrieval for Medical Question Answering**
2604.04593v1 by Byeolhee Kim, Min-Kyung Kim, Young-Hak Kim, Tae-Joon Jeon

Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) grounds large language models in external medical knowledge, yet standard retrievers frequently surface hard negatives that are semantically close to the query but describe clinically distinct conditions. While existing query-expansion methods improve query representation to mitigate ambiguity, they typically focus on enriching target-relevant semantics without an explicit mechanism to selectively suppress specific, clinically plausible hard negatives. This leaves the system prone to retrieving plausible mimics that overshadow the actual diagnosis, particularly when such mimics are dominant within the corpus. We propose Contrastive Hypothesis Retrieval (CHR), a framework inspired by the process of clinical differential diagnosis. CHR generates a target hypothesis $H^+$ for the likely correct answer and a mimic hypothesis $H^-$ for the most plausible incorrect alternative, then scores documents by promoting $H^+$-aligned evidence while penalizing $H^-$-aligned content. Across three medical QA benchmarks and three answer generators, CHR outperforms all five baselines in every configuration, with improvements of up to 10.4 percentage points over the next-best method. On the $n=587$ pooled cases where CHR answers correctly while embedded hypothetical-document query expansion does not, 85.2\% have no shared documents between the top-5 retrieval lists of CHR and of that baseline, consistent with substantive retrieval redirection rather than light re-ranking of the same candidates. By explicitly modeling what to avoid alongside what to find, CHR bridges clinical reasoning with retrieval mechanism design and offers a practical path to reducing hard-negative contamination in medical RAG systems.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）將大型語言模型與外部醫學知識相結合，但標準檢索器經常會出現語義上接近查詢但描述臨床上不同狀況的困難負例。雖然現有的查詢擴展方法改善了查詢表示以減輕歧義，但它們通常專注於豐富目標相關的語義，而沒有明確的機制來選擇性地抑制特定的臨床上合理的困難負例。這使得系統容易檢索到合理的模擬項，這些模擬項會掩蓋實際診斷，特別是當這些模擬項在語料庫中佔主導地位時。我們提出了對比假設檢索（CHR），這是一個受到臨床鑑別診斷過程啟發的框架。CHR 生成一個針對可能正確答案的目標假設 $H^+$ 和一個針對最合理錯誤替代方案的模擬假設 $H^-$，然後通過促進與 $H^+$ 對齊的證據，同時懲罰與 $H^-$ 對齊的內容來對文檔進行打分。在三個醫學問答基準和三個答案生成器中，CHR 在每個配置中都超越了所有五個基準，並在次佳方法上提高了多達 10.4 個百分點。在 $n=587$ 的合併案例中，CHR 正確回答而嵌入的假設文檔查詢擴展則未能做到，85.2\% 的情況下，CHR 的前 5 名檢索列表與該基準之間沒有共享文檔，這與實質性的檢索重定向一致，而不是對相同候選者的輕微重新排序。通過明確建模需要避免的內容和需要尋找的內容，CHR 將臨床推理與檢索機制設計相結合，並提供了一條實際的途徑來減少醫學 RAG 系統中的困難負例污染。

##### **Temporal Inversion for Learning Interval Change in Chest X-Rays**
2604.04563v2 by Hanbin Ko, Kyungmin Jeon, Doowoong Choi, Chang Min Park

Recent advances in vision--language pretraining have enabled strong medical foundation models, yet most analyze radiographs in isolation, overlooking the key clinical task of comparing prior and current images to assess interval change. For chest radiographs (CXRs), capturing interval change is essential, as radiologists must evaluate not only the static appearance of findings but also how they evolve over time. We introduce TILA (Temporal Inversion-aware Learning and Alignment), a simple yet effective framework that uses temporal inversion, reversing image pairs, as a supervisory signal to enhance the sensitivity of existing temporal vision-language models to directional change. TILA integrates inversion-aware objectives across pretraining, fine-tuning, and inference, complementing conventional appearance modeling with explicit learning of temporal order. We also propose a unified evaluation protocol to assess order sensitivity and consistency under temporal inversion, and introduce MS-CXR-Tretrieval, a retrieval evaluation set constructed through a general protocol that can be applied to any temporal CXR dataset. Experiments on public datasets and real-world hospital cohorts demonstrate that TILA consistently improves progression classification and temporal embedding alignment when applied to multiple existing architectures.

摘要：最近在視覺-語言預訓練方面的進展使得強大的醫療基礎模型成為可能，然而大多數模型僅孤立分析放射影像，忽略了比較先前和當前影像以評估時間變化這一關鍵臨床任務。對於胸部放射影像（CXRs），捕捉時間變化是至關重要的，因為放射科醫生必須評估發現的靜態外觀以及它們隨時間的演變。我們介紹了 TILA（時間反轉感知學習與對齊），這是一個簡單但有效的框架，利用時間反轉，即反轉影像對，作為監督信號，以增強現有時間視覺-語言模型對方向性變化的敏感性。TILA 在預訓練、微調和推理過程中整合了反轉感知目標，通過明確學習時間順序來補充傳統的外觀建模。我們還提出了一個統一的評估協議，以評估在時間反轉下的順序敏感性和一致性，並介紹了 MS-CXR-Tretrieval，這是一個通過通用協議構建的檢索評估集，可以應用於任何時間 CXR 數據集。在公共數據集和現實世界醫院隊列上的實驗表明，當 TILA 應用於多個現有架構時，能夠穩定地改善進展分類和時間嵌入對齊。

##### **Reproducibility study on how to find Spurious Correlations, Shortcut Learning, Clever Hans or Group-Distributional non-robustness and how to fix them**
2604.04518v1 by Ole Delzer, Sidney Bender

Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) are increasingly utilized in high-stakes domains like medical diagnostics and autonomous driving where model reliability is critical. However, the research landscape for ensuring this reliability is terminologically fractured across communities that pursue the same goal of ensuring models rely on causally relevant features rather than confounding signals. While frameworks such as distributionally robust optimization (DRO), invariant risk minimization (IRM), shortcut learning, simplicity bias, and the Clever Hans effect all address model failure due to spurious correlations, researchers typically only reference work within their own domains. This reproducibility study unifies these perspectives through a comparative analysis of correction methods under challenging constraints like limited data availability and severe subgroup imbalance. We evaluate recently proposed correction methods based on explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) techniques alongside popular non-XAI baselines using both synthetic and real-world datasets. Findings show that XAI-based methods generally outperform non-XAI approaches, with Counterfactual Knowledge Distillation (CFKD) proving most consistently effective at improving generalization. Our experiments also reveal that the practical application of many methods is hindered by a dependency on group labels, as manual annotation is often infeasible and automated tools like Spectral Relevance Analysis (SpRAy) struggle with complex features and severe imbalance. Furthermore, the scarcity of minority group samples in validation sets renders model selection and hyperparameter tuning unreliable, posing a significant obstacle to the deployment of robust and trustworthy models in safety-critical areas.

摘要：深度神經網絡（DNN）在醫療診斷和自主駕駛等高風險領域的應用越來越普遍，這些領域對模型的可靠性要求極高。<lb/>然而，確保這種可靠性的研究領域在追求相同目標的社群中，術語上卻存在著分歧，這些目標是確保模型依賴於因果相關特徵，而非混淆信號。<lb/>儘管如分佈穩健優化（DRO）、不變風險最小化（IRM）、捷徑學習、簡單性偏見以及聰明漢斯效應等框架都針對由虛假相關性引起的模型失效進行探討，但研究人員通常僅引用自己領域內的工作。<lb/>本次重現性研究通過對在有限數據可用性和嚴重子群不平衡等挑戰性約束下的修正方法進行比較分析，統一了這些觀點。<lb/>我們評估了最近提出的基於可解釋人工智慧（XAI）技術的修正方法，以及使用合成和真實世界數據集的流行非-XAI 基準。<lb/>研究結果顯示，基於XAI的方法通常優於非-XAI 方法，其中反事實知識蒸餾（CFKD）在改善泛化能力方面表現最為一致有效。<lb/>我們的實驗還揭示了許多方法的實際應用受到對群體標籤依賴的限制，因為手動標註通常不可行，而自動化工具如光譜相關性分析（SpRAy）在處理複雜特徵和嚴重不平衡時也面臨困難。<lb/>此外，驗證集中少數群體樣本的稀缺性使得模型選擇和超參數調整變得不可靠，這對於在安全關鍵領域部署穩健和可信的模型構成了重大障礙。

##### **ECG Biometrics with ArcFace-Inception: External Validation on MIMIC and HEEDB**
2604.04485v1 by Arjuna Scagnetto

ECG biometrics has been studied mainly on small cohorts and short inter-session intervals, leaving open how identification behaves under large galleries, external domain shift, and multi-year temporal gaps. We evaluated a 1D
  Inception-v1 model trained with ArcFace on an internal clinical corpus of 164,440 12-lead ECGs from 53,079 patients and tested it on larger cohorts derived from MIMIC-IV-ECG and HEEDB. The study used a unified closed-set leave-one-out
  protocol with Rank@K and TAR@FAR metrics, together with scale, temporal-stress, reranking, and confidence analyses. Under general comparability, the system achieved Rank@1 of 0.9506 on ASUGI-DB, 0.8291 on MIMIC-GC, and 0.6884 on
  HEEDB-GC. In the temporal stress test at constant gallery size, Rank@1 declined from 0.7853 to 0.6433 on MIMIC and from 0.6864 to 0.5560 on HEEDB from 1 to 5 years. Scale analysis on HEEDB showed monotonic degradation as gallery size
  increased and recovery as more examinations per patient became available. On HEEDB-RR, post-hoc reranking further improved retrieval, with AS-norm reaching Rank@1 = 0.8005 from a 0.7765 baseline. ECG identity information therefore
  remains measurable under externally validated large-scale closed-set conditions, but its operational quality is strongly affected by domain heterogeneity, longitudinal drift, gallery size, and second-stage score processing.

摘要：心電圖生物識別主要在小型隊列和短期會話間隔上進行研究，尚未探討在大型資料庫、外部領域轉移和多年時間間隔下的識別行為。我們評估了一個使用 ArcFace 訓練的 1D Inception-v1 模型，該模型基於來自 53,079 名患者的 164,440 份 12 導程心電圖的內部臨床語料庫，並在來自 MIMIC-IV-ECG 和 HEEDB 的更大隊列上進行測試。該研究使用了一個統一的封閉集留一法協議，並結合了 Rank@K 和 TAR@FAR 指標，以及規模、時間壓力、重新排序和信心分析。在一般可比性下，該系統在 ASUGI-DB 上達到了 0.9506 的 Rank@1，在 MIMIC-GC 上為 0.8291，在 HEEDB-GC 上為 0.6884。在恆定畫廊大小的時間壓力測試中，MIMIC 的 Rank@1 從 0.7853 降至 0.6433，而 HEEDB 則從 0.6864 降至 0.5560，時間範圍從 1 年到 5 年。對 HEEDB 的規模分析顯示，隨著畫廊大小的增加，性能單調下降，當每位患者可用的檢查數量增加時則會恢復。在 HEEDB-RR 上，事後重新排序進一步改善了檢索，AS-norm 的 Rank@1 從 0.7765 的基線達到了 0.8005。因此，心電圖身份信息在經外部驗證的大規模封閉集條件下仍然是可測量的，但其操作質量受到領域異質性、縱向漂移、畫廊大小和第二階段分數處理的強烈影響。

##### **MC-GenRef: Annotation-free mammography microcalcification segmentation with generative posterior refinement**
2604.04470v1 by Hyunwoo Cho, Yeeun Kwon, Min Jung Kim, Yangmo Yoo

Microcalcification (MC) analysis is clinically important in screening mammography because clustered puncta can be an early sign of malignancy, yet dense MC segmentation remains challenging: targets are extremely small and sparse, dense pixel-level labels are expensive and ambiguous, and cross-site shift often induces texture-driven false positives and missed puncta in dense tissue. We propose MC-GenRef, a real dense-label-free framework that combines high-fidelity synthetic supervision with test-time generative posterior refinement (TT-GPR). During training, real negative mammogram patches are used as backgrounds, and physically plausible MC patterns are injected through a lightweight image formation model with local contrast modulation and blur, yielding exact image-mask pairs without real dense annotation. Using only these synthetic labeled pairs, MC-GenRef trains a base segmentor and a seed-conditioned rectified-flow (RF) generator that serves as a controllable generative prior. During inference, TT-GPR treats segmentation as approximate posterior inference: it derives a sparse seed from the current prediction, forms seed-consistent RF projections, converts them into case-specific surrogate targets through the frozen segmentor, and iteratively refines the logits with overlap-consistent and edge-aware regularization. On INbreast, the synthetic-only initializer achieved the best Dice without real dense annotations, while TT-GPR improved miss-sensitive performance to Recall and FNR, with strong class-balanced behavior (Bal.Acc., G-Mean). On an external private Yonsei cohort ( n=50 ), TT-GPR consistently improved the synthetic-only initializer under cross-site shift, increasing Dice and Recall while reducing FNR. These results suggest that test-time generative posterior refinement is a practical route to reduce MC misses and improve robustness without additional real dense labeling.

摘要：微鈣化 (MC) 分析在篩檢乳房攝影中具有臨床重要性，因為聚集的點狀物可能是惡性腫瘤的早期徵兆，但密集的 MC 分割仍然具有挑戰性：目標極小且稀疏，密集的像素級標籤昂貴且模糊，跨站點偏移常常導致基於紋理的假陽性和在密集組織中漏掉的點狀物。我們提出了 MC-GenRef，一種真正的無密集標籤框架，結合了高保真度的合成監督和測試時生成後驗精煉 (TT-GPR)。在訓練過程中，真實的負面乳房 X 光片區塊用作背景，並通過一種輕量級的影像形成模型注入物理上合理的 MC 圖案，該模型具有局部對比度調節和模糊效果，從而產生精確的影像-標記對，而不需要真實的密集標註。僅使用這些合成標註對，MC-GenRef 訓練了一個基本分割器和一個種子條件的校正流 (RF) 生成器，該生成器作為可控的生成先驗。在推理過程中，TT-GPR 將分割視為近似後驗推理：它從當前預測中導出一個稀疏種子，形成種子一致的 RF 投影，通過凍結的分割器將其轉換為特定案例的替代目標，並通過重疊一致性和邊緣感知正則化迭代精煉 logits。在 INbreast 上，僅使用合成的初始化器在沒有真實密集標註的情況下達到了最佳的 Dice，而 TT-GPR 改善了對漏檢敏感的性能，提升了召回率和假陰性率 (FNR)，並展現出強大的類別平衡行為 (Bal.Acc., G-Mean)。在一個外部私有的延世隊列 (n=50) 中，TT-GPR 在跨站點偏移下持續改善了僅使用合成的初始化器，增加了 Dice 和召回率，同時降低了 FNR。這些結果表明，測試時生成後驗精煉是一種實用的途徑，可以減少 MC 漏檢並在不需要額外的真實密集標註下提高穩健性。

##### **PSY-STEP: Structuring Therapeutic Targets and Action Sequences for Proactive Counseling Dialogue Systems**
2604.04448v1 by Jihyun Lee, Yejin Min, Yejin Jeon, SungJun Yang, Hyounghun Kim, Gary Geunbae Lee

Cognitive Behavioral Therapy (CBT) aims to identify and restructure automatic negative thoughts pertaining to involuntary interpretations of events, yet existing counseling agents struggle to identify and address them in dialogue settings. To bridge this gap, we introduce STEP, a dataset that models CBT counseling by explicitly reflecting automatic thoughts alongside dynamic, action-level counseling sequences. Using this dataset, we train STEPPER, a counseling agent that proactively elicits automatic thoughts and executes cognitively grounded interventions. To further enhance both decision accuracy and empathic responsiveness, we refine STEPPER through preference learning based on simulated, synthesized counseling sessions. ##### **Domain-Contextualized Inference: A Computable Graph Architecture for Explicit-Domain Reasoning**
2604.04344v2 by Chao Li, Yuru Wang, Chunyi Zhao

We establish a computation-substrate-agnostic inference architecture in which domain is an explicit first-class computational parameter. This produces domain-scoped pruning that reduces per-query search space from O(N) to O(N/K), substrate-independent execution over symbolic, neural, vector, and hybrid substrates, and transparent inference chains where every step carries its evaluative context. The contribution is architectural, not logical. We formalize the computational theory across five dimensions: a five-layer architecture; three domain computation modes including chain indexing, path traversal as Kleisli composition, and vector-guided computation as a substrate transition; a substrate-agnostic interface with three operations Query, Extend, Bridge; reliability conditions C1 to C4 with three failure mode classes; and validation through a PHQ-9 clinical reasoning case study. The computational theory including operational semantics, complexity bounds, monad structure, substrate transitions, and boundary conditions is the contribution of this paper.

摘要：我們建立了一個計算基底無關的推理架構，其中域是一個明確的一級計算參數。這產生了域範圍的修剪，將每個查詢的搜索空間從 O(N) 減少到 O(N/K)，在符號、神經、向量和混合基底上實現基底獨立執行，以及透明的推理鏈，其中每一步都帶有其評估上下文。這項貢獻是架構性的，而非邏輯性的。我們在五個維度上形式化計算理論：一個五層架構；三種域計算模式，包括鏈索引、作為 Kleisli 組合的路徑遍歷，以及作為基底轉換的向量引導計算；一個基底無關的介面，具有三個操作：查詢、擴展、橋接；可靠性條件 C1 到 C4，具有三個故障模式類別；以及通過 PHQ-9 臨床推理案例研究進行驗證。計算理論包括操作語義、複雜性界限、單子結構、基底轉換和邊界條件是本文的貢獻。

##### **Implementing surrogate goals for safer bargaining in LLM-based agents**
2604.04341v1 by Caspar Oesterheld, Maxime Riché, Filip Sondej, Jesse Clifton, Vincent Conitzer

Surrogate goals have been proposed as a strategy for reducing risks from bargaining failures. A surrogate goal is goal that a principal can give an AI agent and that deflects any threats against the agent away from what the principal cares about. For example, one might make one's agent care about preventing money from being burned. Then in bargaining interactions, other agents can threaten to burn their money instead of threatening to spending money to hurt the principal. Importantly, the agent has to care equally about preventing money from being burned as it cares about money being spent to hurt the principal.
  In this paper, we implement surrogate goals in language-model-based agents. In particular, we try to get a language-model-based agent to react to threats of burning money in the same way it would react to "normal" threats. We propose four different methods, using techniques of prompting, fine-tuning, and scaffolding. We evaluate the four methods experimentally. We find that methods based on scaffolding and fine-tuning outperform simple prompting. In particular, fine-tuning and scaffolding more precisely implement the desired behavior w.r.t. threats against the surrogate goal. We also compare the different methods in terms of their side effects on capabilities and propensities in other situations. We find that scaffolding-based methods perform best.

摘要：代理目標被提出作為減少談判失敗風險的一種策略。代理目標是指一個主要方可以給予AI代理的目標，並將任何對代理的威脅轉移到主要方不關心的事物上。例如，人們可能會讓自己的代理關心防止資金被燒毀。然後在談判互動中，其他代理可以威脅燒掉他們的錢，而不是威脅花錢來傷害主要方。重要的是，代理必須同樣關心防止資金被燒毀，與其關心花錢傷害主要方的程度相當。<lb/>在本文中，我們在基於語言模型的代理中實施代理目標。特別是，我們試圖讓基於語言模型的代理對燒錢的威脅做出反應，與其對“正常”威脅的反應相同。我們提出了四種不同的方法，使用提示、微調和支架技術。我們對這四種方法進行了實驗評估。我們發現基於支架和微調的方法優於簡單的提示。特別是，微調和支架更精確地實現了對代理目標威脅的期望行為。我們還比較了不同方法在其他情境中的能力和傾向的副作用。我們發現基於支架的方法表現最佳。

##### **Thermodynamic-Inspired Explainable GeoAI: Uncovering Regime-Dependent Mechanisms in Heterogeneous Spatial Systems**
2604.04339v1 by Sooyoung Lim, Zhenlong Li, Zi-Kui Liu

Modeling spatial heterogeneity and associated critical transitions remains a fundamental challenge in geography and environmental science. While conventional Geographically Weighted Regression (GWR) and deep learning models have improved predictive skill, they often fail to elucidate state-dependent nonlinearities where the functional roles of drivers represent opposing effects across heterogeneous domains. We introduce a thermodynamics-inspired explainable geospatial AI framework that integrates statistical mechanics with graph neural networks. By conceptualizing spatial variability as a thermodynamic competition between system Burden (E) and Capacity (S), our model disentangles the latent mechanisms driving spatial processes. Using three simulation datasets and three real-word datasets across distinct domains (housing markets, mental health prevalence, and wildfire-induced PM2.5 anomalies), we show that the new framework successfully identifies regime-dependent role reversals of predictors that standard baselines miss. Notably, the framework explicitly diagnoses the phase transition into a Burden-dominated regime during the 2023 Canadian wildfire event, distinguishing physical mechanism shifts from statistical outliers. These findings demonstrate that thermodynamic constraints can improve the interpretability of GeoAI while preserving strong predictive performance in complex spatial systems.

摘要：建模空間異質性及其相關的關鍵轉變仍然是地理學和環境科學中的一項基本挑戰。雖然傳統的地理加權回歸（GWR）和深度學習模型提高了預測能力，但它們常常無法闡明狀態依賴的非線性，其中驅動因素的功能角色在異質領域中表現出相反的效果。我們提出了一種受熱力學啟發的可解釋地理空間人工智慧框架，將統計力學與圖神經網絡相結合。通過將空間變異性概念化為系統負擔（E）和容量（S）之間的熱力學競爭，我們的模型解開了驅動空間過程的潛在機制。使用三個模擬數據集和三個來自不同領域的真實世界數據集（住房市場、心理健康流行率和野火引起的PM2.5異常），我們展示了新框架成功識別了標準基準錯過的預測變數的政權依賴角色反轉。值得注意的是，該框架明確診斷了在2023年加拿大野火事件期間進入負擔主導政權的相變，區分了物理機制的變化與統計異常值。這些發現表明，熱力學約束可以改善GeoAI的可解釋性，同時在複雜的空間系統中保持強大的預測性能。

##### **PRIME: Prototype-Driven Multimodal Pretraining for Cancer Prognosis with Missing Modalities**
2604.04999v1 by Kai Yu, Shuang Zhou, Yiran Song, Zaifu Zhan, Jie Peng, Kaixiong Zhou, Tianlong Chen, Feng Xie, Meng Wang, Huazhu Fu, Mingquan Lin, Rui Zhang

Multimodal self-supervised pretraining offers a promising route to cancer prognosis by integrating histopathology whole-slide images, gene expression, and pathology reports, yet most existing approaches require fully paired and complete inputs. In practice, clinical cohorts are fragmented and often miss one or more modalities, limiting both supervised fusion and scalable multimodal pretraining. We propose PRIME, a missing-aware multimodal self-supervised pretraining framework that learns robust and transferable representations from partially observed cohorts. PRIME maps heterogeneous modality embeddings into a unified token space and introduces a shared prototype memory bank for latent-space semantic imputation via patient-level consensus retrieval, producing structurally aligned tokens without reconstructing raw signals. Two complementary pretraining objectives: inter-modality alignment and post-fusion consistency under structured missingness augmentation, jointly learn representations that remain predictive under arbitrary modality subsets. We evaluate PRIME on The Cancer Genome Atlas with label-free pretraining on 32 cancer types and downstream 5-fold evaluation on five cohorts across overall survival prediction, 3-year mortality classification, and 3-year recurrence classification. PRIME achieves the best macro-average performance among all compared methods, reaching 0.653 C-index, 0.689 AUROC, and 0.637 AUROC on the three tasks, respectively, while improving robustness under test-time missingness and supporting parameter-efficient and label-efficient adaptation. These results support missing-aware multimodal pretraining as a practical strategy for prognosis modeling in fragmented clinical data settings.

##### **Good Rankings, Wrong Probabilities: A Calibration Audit of Multimodal Cancer Survival Models**
2604.04239v1 by Sajad Ghawami

Multimodal deep learning models that fuse whole-slide histopathology images with genomic data have achieved strong discriminative performance for cancer survival prediction, as measured by the concordance index. Yet whether the survival probabilities derived from these models - either directly from native outputs or via standard post-hoc reconstruction - are calibrated remains largely unexamined.
  We conduct, to our knowledge, the first systematic fold-level 1-calibration audit of multimodal WSI-genomics survival architectures, evaluating native discrete-time survival outputs (Experiment A: 3 models on TCGA-BRCA) and Breslow-reconstructed survival curves from scalar risk scores (Experiment B: 11 architectures across 5 TCGA cancer types). In Experiment A, all three models fail 1-calibration on a majority of folds (12 of 15 fold-level tests reject after Benjamini-Hochberg correction). Across the full 290 fold-level tests, 166 reject the null of correct calibration at the median event time after Benjamini-Hochberg correction (FDR = 0.05). MCAT achieves C-index 0.817 on GBMLGG yet fails 1-calibration on all five folds.
  Gating-based fusion is associated with better calibration; bilinear and concatenation fusion are not. Post-hoc Platt scaling reduces miscalibration at the evaluated horizon (e.g., MCAT: 5/5 folds failing to 2/5) without affecting discrimination. The concordance index alone is insufficient for evaluating survival models intended for clinical use.

摘要：多模態深度學習模型將全切片組織病理學影像與基因組數據融合，在癌症生存預測方面取得了強大的區別性能，這是通過一致性指數來衡量的。然而，這些模型所衍生的生存概率——無論是直接來自原始輸出還是通過標準的事後重建——是否經過校準仍然大多未被檢驗。<lb/>  
據我們所知，我們進行了首次系統性的折疊級別1校準審計，針對多模態WSI-基因組生存架構，評估原生的離散時間生存輸出（實驗A：3個模型在TCGA-BRCA上）和基於標量風險分數的Breslow重建生存曲線（實驗B：11個架構跨越5個TCGA癌症類型）。在實驗A中，所有三個模型在大多數折疊上都未能通過1校準（15個折疊級別測試中有12個在Benjamini-Hochberg校正後被拒絕）。在全體290個折疊級別測試中，有166個在Benjamini-Hochberg校正後於中位事件時間拒絕正確校準的虛無假設（FDR = 0.05）。MCAT在GBMLGG上達到C指數0.817，但在所有五個折疊上均未能通過1校準。<lb/>  
基於閘控的融合與更好的校準相關；雙線性和串接融合則不然。事後Platt縮放在評估的時間範圍內減少了錯誤校準（例如，MCAT：5/5折疊失敗變為2/5），而不影響區別性。僅僅依賴一致性指數不足以評估用於臨床用途的生存模型。

##### **Robots Need Some Education: On the complexity of learning in evolutionary robotics**
2604.04196v1 by Fuda van Diggelen

Evolutionary Robotics and Robot Learning are two fields in robotics that aim to automatically optimize robot designs. The key difference between them lies in what is being optimized and the time scale involved. Evolutionary Robotics is a field that applies evolutionary computation techniques to evolve the morphologies or controllers, or both. Robot Learning, on the other hand, involves any learning technique aimed at optimizing a robot's controller in a given morphology. In terms of time scales, evolution occurs across multiple generations, whereas learning takes place within the `lifespan' of an individual robot. Integrating Robot Learning with Evolutionary Robotics requires the careful design of suitable learning algorithms in the context of evolutionary robotics. The effects of introducing learning into the evolutionary process are not well-understood and can thus be tricky. This thesis investigates these intricacies and presents several learning algorithms developed for an Evolutionary Robotics context.

摘要：進化機器人學和機器人學習是機器人領域中的兩個分支，旨在自動優化機器人設計。<lb/>它們之間的主要區別在於優化的對象和涉及的時間尺度。<lb/>進化機器人學是一個應用進化計算技術來進化形態或控制器，或兩者兼具的領域。<lb/>另一方面，機器人學習涉及任何旨在優化特定形態下機器人控制器的學習技術。<lb/>在時間尺度方面，進化發生在多代之間，而學習則發生在單個機器人的「壽命」內。<lb/>將機器人學習與進化機器人學結合需要在進化機器人學的背景下仔細設計合適的學習算法。<lb/>將學習引入進化過程的影響尚不完全了解，因此可能會很棘手。<lb/>本論文探討了這些複雜性，並提出了幾種為進化機器人學背景開發的學習算法。

##### **Learning Robust Visual Features in Computed Tomography Enables Efficient Transfer Learning for Clinical Tasks**
2604.04133v1 by Rubén Moreno-Aguado, Alba Magallón, Victor Moreno, Yingying Fang, Guang Yang

There is substantial interest in developing artificial intelligence systems to support radiologists across tasks ranging from segmentation to report generation. Existing computed tomography (CT) foundation models have largely focused on building generalist vision-language systems capable of tasks such as question answering and report generation. However, training reliable vision-language systems requires paired image-text data at a scale that remains unavailable in CT. Moreover, adapting the underlying visual representations to downstream tasks typically requires partial or full backbone fine-tuning, a computationally demanding process inaccessible to many research groups. Instead, foundation models should prioritise learning robust visual representations that enable efficient transfer to new tasks with minimal labelled data and without backbone fine-tuning. We present VoxelFM, a 3D CT foundation model trained with self-distillation using the DINO framework, which learns semantically rich features without language supervision. We evaluated VoxelFM across seven categories of clinically relevant downstream tasks using frozen backbone representations with lightweight probes: classification, regression, survival analysis, instance retrieval, localisation, segmentation, and report generation. VoxelFM matched or outperformed four existing CT foundation models across all task categories. Despite receiving no language supervision during pre-training, VoxelFM surpassed models explicitly trained with language-alignment objectives, including on report generation. Our results indicate that current CT foundation models perform significantly better as feature extractors for lightweight probes rather than as vision encoders for vision-language models. Model weights and training code are publicly available.

摘要：對於開發人工智慧系統以支持放射科醫生在從分割到報告生成等任務方面的工作，存在著相當大的興趣。現有的計算機斷層掃描（CT）基礎模型主要集中於構建能夠執行問題回答和報告生成等任務的通用視覺-語言系統。然而，訓練可靠的視覺-語言系統需要配對的圖像-文本數據，這在CT中仍然無法獲得。此外，將基礎的視覺表示適應於下游任務通常需要部分或完全的主幹微調，這是一個計算需求高的過程，許多研究小組無法獲得。相反，基礎模型應優先學習穩健的視覺表示，以便在最少標記數據的情況下高效轉移到新任務，而無需主幹微調。我們提出了VoxelFM，一個使用DINO框架進行自我蒸餾訓練的3D CT基礎模型，該模型在沒有語言監督的情況下學習語義豐富的特徵。我們使用凍結的主幹表示和輕量級探針，對VoxelFM在七個與臨床相關的下游任務類別上進行了評估：分類、回歸、生存分析、實例檢索、定位、分割和報告生成。VoxelFM在所有任務類別中與四個現有的CT基礎模型相匹配或超越。儘管在預訓練期間未接受語言監督，VoxelFM在報告生成等任務上超越了明確以語言對齊目標進行訓練的模型。我們的結果表明，當前的CT基礎模型在作為輕量級探針的特徵提取器方面表現顯著優於作為視覺-語言模型的視覺編碼器。模型權重和訓練代碼已公開提供。

##### **A Generative Foundation Model for Multimodal Histopathology**
2604.03635v1 by Jinxi Xiang, Mingjie Li, Siyu Hou, Yijiang Chen, Xiangde Luo, Yuanfeng Ji, Xiang Zhou, Ehsan Adeli, Akshay Chaudhari, Curtis P. Langlotz, Kilian M. Pohl, Ruijiang Li

Accurate diagnosis and treatment of complex diseases require integrating histological, molecular, and clinical data, yet in practice these modalities are often incomplete owing to tissue scarcity, assay cost, and workflow constraints. Existing computational approaches attempt to impute missing modalities from available data but rely on task-specific models trained on narrow, single source-target pairs, limiting their generalizability. Here we introduce MuPD (Multimodal Pathology Diffusion), a generative foundation model that embeds hematoxylin and eosin (H&E)-stained histology, molecular RNA profiles, and clinical text into a shared latent space through a diffusion transformer with decoupled cross-modal attention. Pretrained on 100 million histology image patches, 1.6 million text-histology pairs, and 10.8 million RNA-histology pairs spanning 34 human organs, MuPD supports diverse cross-modal synthesis tasks with minimal or no task-specific fine-tuning. For text-conditioned and image-to-image generation, MuPD synthesizes histologically faithful tissue architectures, reducing Fréchet inception distance (FID) scores by 50% relative to domain-specific models and improving few-shot classification accuracy by up to 47% through synthetic data augmentation. For RNA-conditioned histology generation, MuPD reduces FID by 23% compared with the next-best method while preserving cell-type distributions across five cancer types. As a virtual stainer, MuPD translates H&E images to immunohistochemistry and multiplex immunofluorescence, improving average marker correlation by 37% over existing approaches. These results demonstrate that a single, unified generative model pretrained across heterogeneous pathology modalities can substantially outperform specialized alternatives, providing a scalable computational framework for multimodal histopathology.

摘要：準確診斷和治療複雜疾病需要整合組織學、分子和臨床數據，然而在實際操作中，由於組織稀缺、檢測成本和工作流程限制，這些模式往往不完整。現有的計算方法試圖從可用數據中推測缺失的模式，但依賴於在狹窄的單一源-目標對上訓練的特定任務模型，限制了其通用性。在此，我們介紹MuPD（多模態病理擴散），這是一個生成基礎模型，通過具有解耦交叉模態注意力的擴散Transformer，將蘇木精-伊紅（H&E）染色的組織學、分子RNA檔案和臨床文本嵌入到共享潛在空間中。MuPD在1億個組織學圖像補丁、160萬個文本-組織學對和1080萬個RNA-組織學對上進行預訓練，涵蓋34個人類器官，支持多樣的交叉模態合成任務，幾乎不需要或不需要特定任務的微調。對於文本條件和圖像到圖像的生成，MuPD合成了組織學上真實的組織結構，將Fréchet起始距離（FID）分數相對於特定領域模型降低了50%，並通過合成數據增強將少量樣本分類準確率提高了最多47%。對於RNA條件的組織學生成，MuPD將FID相比於次佳方法降低了23%，同時保持了五種癌症類型的細胞類型分佈。作為一個虛擬染色劑，MuPD將H&E圖像轉換為免疫組織化學和多重免疫螢光，將平均標記相關性提高了37%，超過現有方法。這些結果表明，單一的統一生成模型在異質病理模態上進行預訓練，可以顯著超越專門的替代方案，提供一個可擴展的計算框架以進行多模態組織病理學。

##### **A Multimodal Foundation Model of Spatial Transcriptomics and Histology for Biological Discovery and Clinical Prediction**
2604.03630v1 by Jinxi Xiang, Siyu Hou, Yuchen Li, Ryan Quinton, Xiaoming Zhang, Feyisope Eweje, Xiangde Luo, Yijiang Chen, Zhe Li, Colin Bergstrom, Ted Kim, Sierra Willens, Francesca Maria Olguin, Matthew Abikenari, Andrew Heider, Sanjeeth Rajaram, Joel Neal, Maximilian Diehn, Xiang Zhou, Ruijiang Li

We present \textbf{\ours} (\textbf{S}patial \textbf{T}ranscriptomics and hist\textbf{O}logy \textbf{R}epresentation \textbf{M}odel), a foundation model trained on 1.2 million spatially resolved transcriptomic profiles with matched histology across 18 organs. Using a hierarchical architecture integrating morphological features, gene expression, and spatial context, STORM bridges imaging and omics through robust molecular--morphological representations. STORM enhances spatial domain discovery, producing biologically coherent tissue maps, and outperforms existing methods in predicting spatial gene expression from H\&E images across 11 tumor types. The model is platform-agnostic, performing consistently across Visium, Xenium, Visium HD, and CosMx. Applied to 23 independent cohorts comprising 7,245 patients, STORM significantly improves immunotherapy response prediction and prognostication over established biomarkers, providing a scalable framework for spatially informed discovery and clinical precision medicine.

摘要：空間轉錄組學（ST）能夠在解剖學背景下進行基因表達映射，但仍然成本高且通量低。蘇木精-伊紅（H\&E）染色提供了豐富的形態學特徵，但缺乏分子解析度。我們提出了\textbf{\ours}（\textbf{S}patial \textbf{T}ranscriptomics and hist\textbf{O}logy \textbf{R}epresentation \textbf{M}odel），這是一個基於120萬個具有空間解析的轉錄組特徵和18個器官的配對組織學的基礎模型。利用整合形態特徵、基因表達和空間背景的分層架構，STORM通過穩健的分子-形態表示橋接了成像和組學。STORM增強了空間領域的發現，生成生物學上連貫的組織圖，並在預測11種腫瘤類型的H\&E影像中的空間基因表達方面超越了現有方法。該模型是平台無關的，在Visium、Xenium、Visium HD和CosMx上表現一致。應用於23個獨立的隊列，包括7,245名患者，STORM顯著改善了免疫療法反應預測和預後，超越了既有的生物標記，提供了一個可擴展的框架，用於基於空間的發現和臨床精準醫療。

##### **Selective Forgetting for Large Reasoning Models**
2604.03571v1 by Tuan Le, Wei Qian, Mengdi Huai

Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) generate structured chains of thought (CoTs) before producing final answers, making them especially vulnerable to knowledge leakage through intermediate reasoning steps. Yet, the memorization of sensitive information in the training data such as copyrighted and private content has led to ethical and legal concerns. To address these issues, selective forgetting (also known as machine unlearning) has emerged as a potential remedy for LRMs. However, existing unlearning methods primarily target final answers and may degrade the overall reasoning ability of LRMs after forgetting. Additionally, directly applying unlearning on the entire CoTs could degrade the general reasoning capabilities. The key challenge for LRM unlearning lies in achieving precise unlearning of targeted knowledge while preserving the integrity of general reasoning capabilities. To bridge this gap, we in this paper propose a novel LRM unlearning framework that selectively removes sensitive reasoning components while preserving general reasoning capabilities. Our approach leverages multiple LLMs with retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) to analyze CoT traces, identify forget-relevant segments, and replace them with benign placeholders that maintain logical structure. We also introduce a new feature replacement unlearning loss for LRMs, which can simultaneously suppress the probability of generating forgotten content while reinforcing structurally valid replacements. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and medical datasets verify the desired properties of our proposed method.

摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）在生成最終答案之前會產生結構化的思維鏈（CoTs），這使它們在中間推理步驟中尤其容易受到知識洩漏的影響。<lb/>然而，訓練數據中敏感信息的記憶，例如受版權保護和私人內容，已引發倫理和法律問題。<lb/>為了解決這些問題，選擇性遺忘（也稱為機器非學習）已成為LRMs的一種潛在解決方案。<lb/>然而，現有的非學習方法主要針對最終答案，並可能在遺忘後降低LRMs的整體推理能力。<lb/>此外，直接在整個CoTs上應用非學習可能會降低一般推理能力。<lb/>LRM非學習的主要挑戰在於在保留一般推理能力的同時，精確地遺忘目標知識。<lb/>為了填補這一空白，我們在本文中提出了一種新穎的LRM非學習框架，該框架選擇性地移除敏感的推理組件，同時保留一般推理能力。<lb/>我們的方法利用多個帶有檢索增強生成（RAG）的LLMs來分析CoT痕跡，識別與遺忘相關的片段，並用保持邏輯結構的良性佔位符替換它們。<lb/>我們還為LRMs引入了一種新的特徵替換非學習損失，該損失可以同時抑制生成遺忘內容的概率，同時加強結構上有效的替代品。<lb/>在合成和醫療數據集上的廣泛實驗驗證了我們提出的方法的期望特性。

##### **Resource-Conscious Modeling for Next- Day Discharge Prediction Using Clinical Notes**
2604.03498v1 by Ha Na Cho, Sairam Sutari, Alexander Lopez, Hansen Bow, Kai Zheng

Timely discharge prediction is essential for optimizing bed turnover and resource allocation in elective spine surgery units. This study evaluates the feasibility of lightweight, fine-tuned large language models (LLMs) and traditional text-based models for predicting next-day discharge using postoperative clinical notes. We compared 13 models, including TF-IDF with XGBoost and LGBM, and compact LLMs (DistilGPT-2, Bio_ClinicalBERT) fine-tuned via LoRA. TF-IDF with LGBM achieved the best balance, with an F1-score of 0.47 for the discharge class, a recall of 0.51, and the highest AUC-ROC (0.80). While LoRA improved recall in DistilGPT2, overall transformer-based and generative models underperformed. These findings suggest interpretable, resource-efficient models may outperform compact LLMs in real-world, imbalanced clinical prediction tasks.

摘要：及時出院預測對於優化選擇性脊椎手術單位的病床周轉和資源配置至關重要。這項研究評估了輕量級、經過微調的大型語言模型（LLMs）和傳統基於文本的模型在使用術後臨床筆記預測次日出院的可行性。我們比較了13個模型，包括使用XGBoost和LGBM的TF-IDF，以及通過LoRA微調的緊湊型LLMs（DistilGPT-2，Bio_ClinicalBERT）。使用LGBM的TF-IDF達到了最佳平衡，出院類別的F1分數為0.47，召回率為0.51，且AUC-ROC最高（0.80）。雖然LoRA提高了DistilGPT2的召回率，但整體上基於Transformer的生成模型表現不佳。這些發現表明，可解釋的、資源高效的模型在現實世界中不平衡的臨床預測任務中可能超越緊湊型LLMs。

##### **RDFace: A Benchmark Dataset for Rare Disease Facial Image Analysis under Extreme Data Scarcity and Phenotype-Aware Synthetic Generation**
2604.03454v1 by Ganlin Feng, Yuxi Long, Hafsa Ali, Erin Lou, Fahad Butt, Qian Liu, Yang Wang, Pingzhao Hu

Rare diseases often manifest with distinctive facial phenotypes in children, offering valuable diagnostic cues for clinicians and AI-assisted screening systems. However, progress in this field is severely limited by the scarcity of curated, ethically sourced facial data and the high similarity among phenotypes across different conditions. To address these challenges, we introduce RDFace, a curated benchmark dataset comprising 456 pediatric facial images spanning 103 rare genetic conditions (average 4.4 samples per condition). Each ethically verified image is paired with standardized metadata. RDFace enables the development and evaluation of data-efficient AI models for rare disease diagnosis under real-world low-data constraints. We benchmark multiple pretrained vision backbones using cross-validation and explore synthetic augmentation with DreamBooth and FastGAN. Generated images are filtered via facial landmark similarity to maintain phenotype fidelity and merged with real data, improving diagnostic accuracy by up to 13.7% in ultra-low-data regimes. To assess semantic validity, phenotype descriptions generated by a vision-language model from real and synthetic images achieve a report similarity score of 0.84. RDFace establishes a transparent, benchmark-ready dataset for equitable rare disease AI research and presents a scalable framework for evaluating both diagnostic performance and the integrity of synthetic medical imagery.

摘要：罕見疾病在兒童中常以獨特的面部表現型顯現，為臨床醫生和人工智慧輔助篩檢系統提供了寶貴的診斷線索。<lb/>然而，這一領域的進展受到策劃的、倫理來源的面部數據稀缺以及不同病症之間表現型高度相似的嚴重限制。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們推出了RDFace，一個策劃的基準數據集，包含456張涵蓋103種罕見遺傳病的兒童面部圖像（每種病症平均4.4個樣本）。<lb/>每張經過倫理驗證的圖像都配有標準化的元數據。<lb/>RDFace使得在現實世界低數據限制下，開發和評估數據高效的人工智慧模型以進行罕見疾病診斷成為可能。<lb/>我們使用交叉驗證基準多個預訓練的視覺骨幹，並探索使用DreamBooth和FastGAN的合成增強。<lb/>生成的圖像通過面部標誌相似性進行過濾，以保持表現型的真實性，並與真實數據合併，在超低數據環境中提高診斷準確性達13.7%。<lb/>為了評估語義有效性，從真實和合成圖像生成的表現型描述，由視覺-語言模型產生的報告相似性得分為0.84。<lb/>RDFace建立了一個透明的、準備好的基準數據集，以促進公平的罕見疾病人工智慧研究，並提供了一個可擴展的框架來評估診斷性能和合成醫學影像的完整性。

##### **PR3DICTR: A modular AI framework for medical 3D image-based detection and outcome prediction**
2604.03203v1 by Daniel C. MacRae, Luuk van der Hoek, Robert van der Wal, Suzanne P. M. de Vette, Hendrike Neh, Baoqiang Ma, Peter M. A. van Ooijen, Lisanne V. van Dijk

Three-dimensional medical image data and computer-aided decision making, particularly using deep learning, are becoming increasingly important in the medical field.
